<file path="app/actions/QuyenHanQuyTrinhMau.ts">
'use server';

import postgres from 'postgres';
import { createServerClient } from '@supabase/ssr';
import { cookies } from 'next/headers';

const sql = postgres(process.env.DATABASE_URL!, { ssl: 'require' });

async function requireAuth() {
    const cookieStore = await cookies();
    const supabase = createServerClient(
        process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL!,
        process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY!,
        { cookies: { get(name: string) { return cookieStore.get(name)?.value }, set() {}, remove() {} } }
    );
    const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
    if (!user) throw new Error("Unauthorized");
    return user.id; // Tr·∫£ v·ªÅ ID c·ªßa user (Admin)
}

// 1. L·∫§Y DANH S√ÅCH
export async function getQuyTrinhMauAction(page: number, pageSize: number, search: string) {
    try {
        await requireAuth();
        
        let query = `
            SELECT 
                qt.id, qt.tao_luc,
                ns.ho_ten as nguoi_tao,
                
                -- Th√¥ng tin t·ª´ b·∫£ng tac_pham_trung_bay
                tp.kich_thuoc, tp.chat_lieu, tp.ky_thuat_thuc_hien,
                
                -- Th√¥ng tin t·ª´ b·∫£ng mau_thiet_ke
                mtk.mo_ta as ten_mau_thiet_ke, mtk.hinh_anh

            FROM "quy_trinh_san_xuat_mau" qt
            JOIN "tac_pham_trung_bay" tp ON qt.tac_pham_trung_bay = tp.id
            LEFT JOIN "mau_thiet_ke" mtk ON tp.mau_thiet_ke = mtk.id
            LEFT JOIN "nhan_su" ns ON qt.nguoi_tao = ns.id
            WHERE 1=1
        `;
        
        const params: any[] = [];
        if (search) {
            query += ` AND (mtk.mo_ta ILIKE $1 OR tp.chat_lieu ILIKE $1)`;
            params.push(`%${search}%`);
        }

        query += ` ORDER BY qt.tao_luc DESC LIMIT ${pageSize} OFFSET ${(page - 1) * pageSize}`;
        
        const data = await sql.unsafe(query, params);
        return { success: true, data: Array.from(data) };
    } catch (error: any) { return { success: false, error: error.message }; }
}

// 2. T·∫†O M·ªöI (Insert v√†o c·∫£ 2 b·∫£ng)
export async function createQuyTrinhMauAction(data: any) {
    try {
        const userId = await requireAuth();

        await sql.begin(async sql => {
            // B∆∞·ªõc 1: T·∫°o T√°c Ph·∫©m Tr∆∞ng B√†y tr∆∞·ªõc
            const [tp] = await sql`
                INSERT INTO "tac_pham_trung_bay" (mau_thiet_ke, kich_thuoc, chat_lieu, ky_thuat_thuc_hien)
                VALUES (${data.mau_thiet_ke}, ${data.kich_thuoc}, ${data.chat_lieu}, ${data.ky_thuat_thuc_hien})
                RETURNING id
            `;

            // B∆∞·ªõc 2: T·∫°o Quy Tr√¨nh li√™n k·∫øt v·ªõi T√°c ph·∫©m v·ª´a t·∫°o
            await sql`
                INSERT INTO "quy_trinh_san_xuat_mau" (nguoi_tao, tac_pham_trung_bay, tao_luc)
                VALUES (${userId}, ${tp.id}, now())
            `;
        });

        return { success: true };
    } catch (error: any) { return { success: false, error: error.message }; }
}

// 3. X√ìA
export async function deleteQuyTrinhMauAction(id: string) {
    try {
        await requireAuth();
        // Do c√≥ ON DELETE CASCADE, ch·ªâ c·∫ßn x√≥a quy tr√¨nh l√† t√°c ph·∫©m ƒëi theo (ho·∫∑c ng∆∞·ª£c l·∫°i t√πy thi·∫øt k·∫ø DB, ·ªü ƒë√¢y x√≥a b·∫£ng cha tr∆∞·ªõc)
        await sql`DELETE FROM "quy_trinh_san_xuat_mau" WHERE id = ${id}`;
        return { success: true };
    } catch (error: any) { return { success: false, error: error.message }; }
}

// 4. L·∫§Y OPTION M·∫™U THI·∫æT K·∫æ (Cho dropdown)
export async function getMauThietKeOptionsAction() {
    try {
        await requireAuth();
        const data = await sql`SELECT id, mo_ta as label, hinh_anh FROM "mau_thiet_ke" ORDER BY tao_luc DESC`;
        return { success: true, data: Array.from(data) };
    } catch (error: any) { return { success: false, error: error.message }; }
}

<file path="app/actions/QuyenHanTacPham.ts">
'use server';

import postgres from 'postgres';
import { createServerClient } from '@supabase/ssr';
import { cookies } from 'next/headers';

const sql = postgres(process.env.DATABASE_URL!, { ssl: 'require' });

async function requireAuth() {
    const cookieStore = await cookies();
    const supabase = createServerClient(
        process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL!,
        process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY!,
        { cookies: { get(name: string) { return cookieStore.get(name)?.value }, set() {}, remove() {} } }
    );
    const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
    if (!user) throw new Error("Unauthorized");
    return user.id;
}

// 1. L·∫§Y DANH S√ÅCH T√ÅC PH·∫®M
export async function getTacPhamDataAction(page: number, pageSize: number, search: string, filterChatLieu: string) {
    try {
        await requireAuth();
        
        let query = `
            SELECT 
                tp.id, tp.kich_thuoc, tp.chat_lieu, tp.ky_thuat_thuc_hien,
                mtk.mo_ta as ten_mau_thiet_ke, 
                mtk.hinh_anh,
                tp.mau_thiet_ke as mau_thiet_ke_id
            FROM "tac_pham_trung_bay" tp
            JOIN "mau_thiet_ke" mtk ON tp.mau_thiet_ke = mtk.id
            WHERE 1=1
        `;
        
        const params: any[] = [];
        let paramCount = 1;

        if (search) {
            query += ` AND (mtk.mo_ta ILIKE $${paramCount})`;
            params.push(`%${search}%`);
            paramCount++;
        }

        if (filterChatLieu && filterChatLieu !== 'all') {
            query += ` AND tp.chat_lieu = $${paramCount}`;
            params.push(filterChatLieu);
            paramCount++;
        }

        query += ` ORDER BY tp.id DESC LIMIT ${pageSize} OFFSET ${(page - 1) * pageSize}`;
        
        const data = await sql.unsafe(query, params);
        return { success: true, data: Array.from(data) };
    } catch (error: any) { return { success: false, error: error.message }; }
}

// 2. T·∫†O T√ÅC PH·∫®M M·ªöI
export async function createTacPhamAction(data: any) {
    try {
        await requireAuth();
        await sql`
            INSERT INTO "tac_pham_trung_bay" (mau_thiet_ke, kich_thuoc, chat_lieu, ky_thuat_thuc_hien)
            VALUES (${data.mau_thiet_ke}, ${data.kich_thuoc}, ${data.chat_lieu}, ${data.ky_thuat_thuc_hien})
        `;
        return { success: true };
    } catch (error: any) { return { success: false, error: error.message }; }
}

// 3. C·∫¨P NH·∫¨T T√ÅC PH·∫®M
export async function updateTacPhamAction(id: string, data: any) {
    try {
        await requireAuth();
        await sql`
            UPDATE "tac_pham_trung_bay"
            SET mau_thiet_ke = ${data.mau_thiet_ke},
                kich_thuoc = ${data.kich_thuoc},
                chat_lieu = ${data.chat_lieu},
                ky_thuat_thuc_hien = ${data.ky_thuat_thuc_hien}
            WHERE id = ${id}
        `;
        return { success: true };
    } catch (error: any) { return { success: false, error: error.message }; }
}

// 4. X√ìA T√ÅC PH·∫®M
export async function deleteTacPhamAction(id: string) {
    try {
        await requireAuth();
        await sql`DELETE FROM "tac_pham_trung_bay" WHERE id = ${id}`;
        return { success: true };
    } catch (error: any) { return { success: false, error: error.message }; }
}

<file path="app/actions/SanXuatAction.ts">
"use server";

import { createServerClient } from "@supabase/ssr";
import { cookies } from "next/headers";

// 1. L·∫§Y DANH S√ÅCH C√îNG VI·ªÜC TRONG NG√ÄY
export async function getKeHoachSanXuat() {
  const cookieStore = await cookies();
  const supabase = createServerClient(
    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL!,
    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY!,
    {
      cookies: {
        get(name: string) { return cookieStore.get(name)?.value; },
      },
    }
  );

  try {
    // L·∫•y vi·ªác t·ª´ b·∫£ng K·∫ø Ho·∫°ch, Join v·ªõi ƒê∆°n H√†ng ƒë·ªÉ bi·∫øt vi·ªác n√†y c·ªßa ƒë∆°n n√†o
    const { data, error } = await supabase
      .from("ke_hoach_san_xuat")
      .select(`
        *,
        chi_tiet_don_hang: chi_tiet_don_hang_id (
            so_luong,
            kich_thuoc,
            ghi_chu_san_pham,
            mau_thiet_ke: mau_thiet_ke_id ( id, mo_ta, hinh_anh ),
            don_hang: don_hang_id ( ma_don, trang_thai )
        ),
        nguoi_thuc_hien: nguoi_thuc_hien_id ( ho_ten, hinh_anh )
      `)
      .order("tao_luc", { ascending: false });

    if (error) throw error;
    return { success: true, data };
  } catch (error: any) {
    console.error("L·ªói l·∫•y k·∫ø ho·∫°ch SX:", error);
    return { success: false, error: error.message };
  }
}

// 2. TH·ª¢ NH·∫¨N VI·ªÜC (CHUY·ªÇN T·ª™ 'cho_viec' -> 'dang_lam')
export async function nhanViecAction(idViec: string) {
  const cookieStore = await cookies();
  const supabase = createServerClient(
    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL!,
    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY!,
    {
      cookies: {
        get(name: string) { return cookieStore.get(name)?.value; },
      },
    }
  );

  try {
    // L·∫•y user hi·ªán t·∫°i
    const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
    if (!user) throw new Error("Ch∆∞a ƒëƒÉng nh·∫≠p");

    // L·∫•y ID nh√¢n s·ª± t·ª´ b·∫£ng nhan_su
    const { data: ns } = await supabase
        .from('nhan_su')
        .select('id')
        .eq('email', user.email)
        .single();
    
    if (!ns) throw new Error("Kh√¥ng t√¨m th·∫•y h·ªì s∆° nh√¢n s·ª±");

    // Update
    const { error } = await supabase
      .from("ke_hoach_san_xuat")
      .update({
        trang_thai: "dang_lam",
        nguoi_thuc_hien_id: ns.id,
        bat_dau_luc: new Date().toISOString()
      })
      .eq("id", idViec);

    if (error) throw error;
    return { success: true };
  } catch (error: any) {
    return { success: false, error: error.message };
  }
}

// 3. HO√ÄN TH√ÄNH VI·ªÜC (CHUY·ªÇN T·ª™ 'dang_lam' -> 'hoan_thanh')
export async function hoanThanhViecAction(idViec: string) {
  const cookieStore = await cookies();
  const supabase = createServerClient(
    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL!,
    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY!,
    {
      cookies: {
        get(name: string) { return cookieStore.get(name)?.value; },
      },
    }
  );

  try {
    const { error } = await supabase
      .from("ke_hoach_san_xuat")
      .update({
        trang_thai: "hoan_thanh",
        ket_thuc_luc: new Date().toISOString()
      })
      .eq("id", idViec);

    if (error) throw error;
    return { success: true };
  } catch (error: any) {
    return { success: false, error: error.message };
  }
}
</file>

export const getKhachHangList = cache(async (): Promise<KhachHang[]> => {
  const supabase = await createClient();
  
  const { data, error } = await supabase
    .from('khach_hang')
    .select('*')
    .order('tao_luc', { ascending: false });

  if (error) {
    console.error("L·ªói l·∫•y danh s√°ch kh√°ch h√†ng:", error);
    return [];
  }

  return (data || []) as KhachHang[];
});

import { ManagerConfig, FieldConfig } from "../types";

    getQuyTrinhMauAction,

    getMauThietKeOptionsAction

export interface QuyTrinhSanXuatMau {
    id: string;
    ten_mau_thiet_ke: string;
    hinh_anh?: string;
    kich_thuoc: string;
    chat_lieu: string;
    ky_thuat_thuc_hien: string;
    nguoi_tao: string;
    tao_luc: string;
    // D·ªØ li·ªáu ƒë·ªÉ g·ª≠i form
    mau_thiet_ke?: string;

// C√ÅC GI√Å TR·ªä SINGLE CHOICE THEO Y√äU C·∫¶U
const KICH_THUOC_OPTS = ['20x30', '30x40', '40x60'];
const CHAT_LIEU_OPTS = ['G·∫°o nguy√™n h·∫°t 100%', 'G·∫°o - T·∫•m - C√°m'];
const KY_THUAT_OPTS = ['Th·ªß c√¥ng 100%', 'In UV', 'B√°n th·ªß c√¥ng'];

const fields: FieldConfig[] = [
    {
        key: 'hinh_anh',
        label: '·∫¢nh m·∫´u',
        type: 'image',
        showInForm: false, 
        showInDetail: true,
        showInCard: true,
    },
    {
        key: 'mau_thiet_ke', // ID m·∫´u thi·∫øt k·∫ø
        label: 'Ch·ªçn M·∫´u Thi·∫øt K·∫ø',
        type: 'select-add',
        placeholder: 'Ch·ªçn m·∫´u...',
        required: true,
        icon: Palette,
        showInCard: false,

             const res = await getMauThietKeOptionsAction();
             // üü¢ ƒê√£ fix ·ªü types.ts n√™n gi·ªù return m·∫£ng object tho·∫£i m√°i
             return res.data?.map((m: any) => ({ value: m.id, label: m.label })) || [];
        }
    },
    {
        key: 'ten_mau_thiet_ke', // T√™n hi·ªÉn th·ªã
        label: 'T√™n T√°c Ph·∫©m',
        type: 'text',
        showInForm: false,
        icon: Palette,
    },
    {
        key: 'kich_thuoc',
        label: 'K√≠ch Th∆∞·ªõc',
        type: 'select',
        options: KICH_THUOC_OPTS, // 20x30, 30x40...
        required: true,
        icon: Ruler,
    },
    {
        key: 'chat_lieu',
        label: 'Ch·∫•t Li·ªáu',
        type: 'select',
        options: CHAT_LIEU_OPTS, // G·∫°o...
        required: true,
        icon: Layers,
    },
    {
        key: 'ky_thuat_thuc_hien',
        label: 'K·ªπ Thu·∫≠t Th·ª±c Hi·ªán',
        type: 'select',
        options: KY_THUAT_OPTS, // Th·ªß c√¥ng...
        required: true,
        icon: PenTool,

        label: 'Ng∆∞·ªùi T·∫°o',
        type: 'readonly',
        showInForm: false,

    }

    fetchList: async (page: number, limit: number, search: string) => {
        const res = await getQuyTrinhMauAction(page, limit, search);
        return { 
            success: res.success, 
            // üü¢ S·ª¨A L·ªñI 2: √âp ki·ªÉu qua unknown ƒë·ªÉ tr√°nh l·ªói "overlap" c·ªßa TS
            data: res.data as unknown as QuyTrinhSanXuatMau[], 
            error: res.error 
        };
    },
    create: async (data: any) => {
        const res = await createQuyTrinhMauAction(data);
        return { 
            success: res.success, 
            // üü¢ S·ª¨A L·ªñI 3: Tr·∫£ v·ªÅ null h·ª£p l·ªá v√¨ types.ts ƒë√£ cho ph√©p data?
            data: null, 
            error: res.error 
        };
    },
    delete: async (id: string) => {
        const res = await deleteQuyTrinhMauAction(id);
        return { success: res.success, error: res.error };
    }
};

export function createQuyTrinhMauConfig(): ManagerConfig<QuyTrinhSanXuatMau> {

        entityName: 'quy tr√¨nh m·∫´u',
        entityNamePlural: 'quy tr√¨nh s·∫£n xu·∫•t m·∫´u',
        idField: 'id',
        fields,
        cardConfig: {
            avatarField: 'hinh_anh',

            subtitleField: 'chat_lieu',
            infoFields: [
                { field: 'kich_thuoc', icon: Ruler },
                { field: 'ky_thuat_thuc_hien', icon: PenTool }
            ]
        },
        filterTabs: [{ id: 'all', label: 'T·∫§T C·∫¢' }],
        detailTabs: [{ id: 'info', label: 'TH√îNG TIN' }],
        actions: {
            allowView: true,
            allowEdit: true, // Cho ph√©p t·∫°o
            allowDelete: true,
        },
        dataSource,
        searchFields: ['ten_mau_thiet_ke'],
    };
}

"use client";

import React, { useState, useEffect, useMemo, useCallback } from "react";
import { Trash2 } from "lucide-react";
import { KhungDanhSach, KhungForm, KhungChiTiet } from "@/app/components/cacchucnang/KhungGiaoDienChucNang";
import ConfirmDialog from "@/app/components/ConfirmDialog";
import { createQuyTrinhMauConfig, QuyTrinhSanXuatMau } from "./config";

// T·∫≠n d·ª•ng l·∫°i ViecMauList ƒë·ªÉ hi·ªÉn th·ªã Grid (v√¨ c·∫•u tr√∫c na n√° nhau)
import ViecMauList from "../viecmau/ViecMauList"; 

export default function QuyTrinhSanXuatMauChucNang() {
    const config = createQuyTrinhMauConfig();
    
    // State
    const [items, setItems] = useState<QuyTrinhSanXuatMau[]>([]);
    const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
    const [viewMode, setViewMode] = useState<'list' | 'form' | 'detail'>('list');
    const [selectedItem, setSelectedItem] = useState<QuyTrinhSanXuatMau | null>(null);
    const [confirmDelete, setConfirmDelete] = useState<{ show: boolean; ids: string[] }>({ show: false, ids: [] });

    // Fetch
    const fetchData = useCallback(async () => {
        setLoading(true);
        try {
            const res = await config.dataSource!.fetchList!(1, 100, "", "");
            if (res.success && res.data) setItems(res.data);
        } catch(e) { console.error(e); }
        finally { setLoading(false); }
    }, []);

    useEffect(() => { fetchData(); }, [fetchData]);

    // Handlers
    const handleDelete = async () => {
        if(confirmDelete.ids.length > 0) {
            await config.dataSource!.delete!(confirmDelete.ids[0]);
            setConfirmDelete({ show: false, ids: [] });
            fetchData();
            setViewMode('list');
        }
    };

    return (
        <div className="h-full">
            {/* LIST VIEW */}
            {viewMode === 'list' && (
                <KhungDanhSach
                    data={items}
                    tabDefs={[{ id: 'all', label: 'T·∫§T C·∫¢', count: items.length }]}
                    onAdd={() => { setSelectedItem(null); setViewMode('form'); }}
                    showAddButton={true}
                    loading={loading}
                    onSearch={() => {}} // Placeholder
                >
                    {/* D√πng t·∫°m UI List c·ªßa ViecMau v√¨ n√≥ ƒë·∫πp v√† kh·ªõp */}
                    <ViecMauList 
                        items={items.map(i => ({
                            id: i.id,
                            mo_ta: i.ten_mau_thiet_ke,
                            phan_loai: i.kich_thuoc + ' - ' + i.chat_lieu,
                            hinh_anh: i.hinh_anh,
                            nguoi_tao: i.nguoi_tao,
                            tao_luc: i.tao_luc,
                            phan_loai_normalized: ''
                        }))}
                        bulkMode={false}
                        selectedIds={new Set()}
                        onToggleSelect={() => {}}
                        onClickItem={(item) => {
                            // Map l·∫°i item ƒë·ªÉ xem chi ti·∫øt
                            const original = items.find(i => i.id === item.id);
                            if(original) {
                                setSelectedItem(original);
                                setViewMode('detail');
                            }
                        }}
                    />
                </KhungDanhSach>
            )}

            {/* FORM VIEW */}
            {viewMode === 'form' && (
                <KhungForm
                    title="T·∫†O QUY TR√åNH M·∫™U M·ªöI"
                    onClose={() => setViewMode('list')}
                    action={{
                        validate: (data) => {
                            if(!data.mau_thiet_ke) return "Ch∆∞a ch·ªçn m·∫´u thi·∫øt k·∫ø";
                            if(!data.kich_thuoc) return "Ch∆∞a ch·ªçn k√≠ch th∆∞·ªõc";
                            if(!data.chat_lieu) return "Ch∆∞a ch·ªçn ch·∫•t li·ªáu";
                            if(!data.ky_thuat_thuc_hien) return "Ch∆∞a ch·ªçn k·ªπ thu·∫≠t";
                            return null;
                        },
                        onSave: async (data) => config.dataSource!.create!(data),
                        onSuccess: () => { fetchData(); }
                    }}
                >
                   {/* Form t·ª± ƒë·ªông render d·ª±a tr√™n config.fields */}
                   <div className="grid gap-4">
                        {config.fields.map(field => {
                            if (!field.showInForm && field.key !== 'mau_thiet_ke' && field.key !== 'kich_thuoc' && field.key !== 'chat_lieu' && field.key !== 'ky_thuat_thuc_hien') return null;
                            
                            // Render th·ªß c√¥ng ƒë∆°n gi·∫£n ho·∫∑c d√πng component FormField n·∫øu c√≥
                            // ·ªû ƒë√¢y t√¥i gi·∫£ l·∫≠p ƒë∆°n gi·∫£n:
                            return (
                                <div key={field.key}>
                                    <label className="text-xs text-gray-400 font-bold uppercase mb-1 block">{field.label}</label>
                                    
                                    {field.type === 'select' ? (
                                        <select name={field.key} className="w-full bg-[#1a1a1a] border border-white/10 p-3 rounded text-white" defaultValue="">
                                            <option value="" disabled>Ch·ªçn...</option>
                                            {field.options?.map((opt: any) => (
                                                <option key={opt} value={opt}>{opt}</option>
                                            ))}
                                        </select>
                                    ) : field.type === 'select-add' ? (
                                        // Component select async ph·ª©c t·∫°p h∆°n, ·ªü ƒë√¢y t√¥i render input th∆∞·ªùng demo
                                         <p className="text-red-500 text-xs">C·∫ßn component Select Async cho {field.label}</p>
                                    ) : (
                                        <input name={field.key} type="text" className="w-full bg-[#1a1a1a] border border-white/10 p-3 rounded text-white" />
                                    )}
                                </div>
                            )
                        })}
                   </div>
                   {/* L∆∞u √Ω: ƒê·ªÉ form ho·∫°t ƒë·ªông 100% c·∫ßn t√≠ch h·ª£p v√†o KhungForm chu·∫©n. 
                       Code tr√™n ƒëang demo logic k·∫øt n·ªëi. */}
                </KhungForm>
            )}

            {/* DETAIL VIEW */}
            {viewMode === 'detail' && selectedItem && (
                 <KhungChiTiet
                    data={selectedItem}
                    onClose={() => setViewMode('list')}
                    title={selectedItem.ten_mau_thiet_ke}
                    tabDefs={[{ id: 'info', label: 'TH√îNG TIN' }]}
                    showDeleteButton={true}
                    onDelete={() => setConfirmDelete({ show: true, ids: [selectedItem.id] })}
                 >
                    <div className="p-4 space-y-4">
                        <div className="aspect-video bg-[#1a1a1a] rounded overflow-hidden">
                            <img src={selectedItem.hinh_anh} className="w-full h-full object-contain" />
                        </div>
                        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
                            <InfoBox label="K√≠ch th∆∞·ªõc" value={selectedItem.kich_thuoc} />
                            <InfoBox label="Ch·∫•t li·ªáu" value={selectedItem.chat_lieu} />
                            <InfoBox label="K·ªπ thu·∫≠t" value={selectedItem.ky_thuat_thuc_hien} />
                            <InfoBox label="Ng∆∞·ªùi t·∫°o" value={selectedItem.nguoi_tao} />
                        </div>
                    </div>
                 </KhungChiTiet>
            )}

            <ConfirmDialog 
                isOpen={confirmDelete.show}
                title="X√ìA QUY TR√åNH?"
                message="B·∫°n c√≥ ch·∫Øc ch·∫Øn mu·ªën x√≥a quy tr√¨nh n√†y kh√¥ng?"
                onConfirm={handleDelete}
                onCancel={() => setConfirmDelete({ show: false, ids: [] })}
            />
        </div>
    );
}

function InfoBox({ label, value }: any) {
    return (
        <div className="bg-[#1a1a1a] p-3 rounded border border-white/5">
            <div className="text-[10px] text-gray-500 uppercase font-bold">{label}</div>
            <div className="text-white font-medium">{value}</div>
        </div>
    );
}

<file path="app/components/cacchucnang/sanxuat/dal.ts">
import { cache } from 'react';
import { createClient } from '@/app/ThuVien/supabase/server';

// --- DTO: ƒê·ªãnh nghƒ©a d·ªØ li·ªáu Task chu·∫©n ---
export interface TaskDTO {
  id: string;
  // C√°c tr∆∞·ªùng chu·∫©n m·ªõi (English)
  title: string;
  status: 'cho_viec' | 'dang_lam' | 'hoan_thanh';
  duration: number;
  productNote: string;
  orderCode: string;
  designImage?: string;
  workerName?: string;
  
  // C√°c tr∆∞·ªùng Legacy (Ti·∫øng Vi·ªát) ƒë·ªÉ t∆∞∆°ng th√≠ch UI c≈©
  ten_viec: string; 
  trang_thai: string;
  thoi_gian_du_kien: number;
  thu_tu: number;
  
  // C√°c object quan h·ªá
  chi_tiet_don_hang: any;
  nguoi_thuc_hien: any;
}

// --- H√†m l·∫•y DATA cho CH·ª®C NƒÇNG S·∫¢N XU·∫§T ---
// D√πng cache() c·ªßa React ƒë·ªÉ Server kh√¥ng query l·∫∑p l·∫°i
export const getProductionTasks = cache(async (): Promise<TaskDTO[]> => {
  const supabase = await createClient();

  const { data, error } = await supabase
    .from('ke_hoach_san_xuat')
    .select(`
      id, ten_viec, trang_thai, thoi_gian_du_kien, thu_tu,
      chi_tiet_don_hang (
        ghi_chu_san_pham,
        don_hang ( ma_don ),
        mau_thiet_ke ( hinh_anh )
      ),
      nguoi_thuc_hien ( ho_ten )
    `)
    .order('thu_tu', { ascending: true });

  if (error || !data) return [];

  // Map d·ªØ li·ªáu: ƒê·∫£m b·∫£o c√≥ ƒë·ªß c·∫£ tr∆∞·ªùng c≈© v√† m·ªõi
  return data.map((item: any) => ({
    id: item.id,
    
    // Mapping tr∆∞·ªùng m·ªõi
    title: item.ten_viec,
    status: item.trang_thai,
    duration: item.thoi_gian_du_kien,
    productNote: item.chi_tiet_don_hang?.ghi_chu_san_pham || 'S·∫£n ph·∫©m chu·∫©n',
    orderCode: item.chi_tiet_don_hang?.don_hang?.ma_don || 'N/A',
    designImage: item.chi_tiet_don_hang?.mau_thiet_ke?.hinh_anh,
    workerName: item.nguoi_thuc_hien?.ho_ten,
    
    // Mapping tr∆∞·ªùng c≈© (Gi·ªØ nguy√™n t√™n c·ªôt DB)
    ten_viec: item.ten_viec,
    trang_thai: item.trang_thai,
    thoi_gian_du_kien: item.thoi_gian_du_kien,
    thu_tu: item.thu_tu,
    
    // Gi·ªØ nguy√™n relations
    chi_tiet_don_hang: item.chi_tiet_don_hang,
    nguoi_thuc_hien: item.nguoi_thuc_hien
  }));
});
</file>

<file path="app/components/cacchucnang/sanxuat/SanXuatChucNang.tsx">
"use client";

import React, { useState, useEffect, useMemo, useCallback } from "react";
import { KhungDanhSach } from "@/app/components/cacchucnang/KhungGiaoDienChucNang";
import { filterTabs, dataSource } from "./config";
import SanXuatList from "./SanXuatList";
import SanXuatDetail from "./SanXuatDetail";

// Define Type ƒë·ªÉ tr√°nh l·ªói TS
import { TaskDTO } from "./dal";

interface Props {
  className?: string;
  // üü¢ NH·∫¨N INITIAL DATA T·ª™ SERVER
  initialData?: any[]; 
}

export default function SanXuatChucNang({ className = "", initialData = [] }: Props) {
  // State
  // üü¢ D√πng initialData kh·ªüi t·∫°o State -> HI·ªÜN NGAY L·∫¨P T·ª®C
  const [items, setItems] = useState<any[]>(initialData);
  
  // üü¢ M·∫∑c ƒë·ªãnh kh√¥ng loading v√¨ ƒë√£ c√≥ data
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  
  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState("all"); 
  const [searchTerm, setSearchTerm] = useState("");
  const [selectedItem, setSelectedItem] = useState<any | null>(null);

  // Fetch Data (Ch·ªâ d√πng cho Auto-refresh)
  const fetchData = useCallback(async (isBackground = false) => {
    if (!isBackground) setLoading(true);
    try {
      const res = await dataSource.fetchList();
      if (res.success) setItems(res.data || []);
    } catch (e) {
      console.error(e);
    } finally {
      if (!isBackground) setLoading(false);
    }
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    // üü¢ B·ªé fetchData() l√∫c mount
    
    // Ch·ªâ gi·ªØ Auto refresh (30s/l·∫ßn)
    const interval = setInterval(() => fetchData(true), 30000);
    return () => clearInterval(interval);
  }, [fetchData]);

  // Filter Logic
  const filteredList = useMemo(() => {
    let result = items;
    if (activeTab !== "all") {
      result = result.filter((i) => i.trang_thai === activeTab);
    }
    if (searchTerm) {
      const term = searchTerm.toLowerCase();
      result = result.filter((i) => 
        i.ten_viec.toLowerCase().includes(term) || 
        i.chi_tiet_don_hang?.don_hang?.ma_don.toLowerCase().includes(term)
      );
    }
    return result;
  }, [items, activeTab, searchTerm]);

  // Handle Actions
  const handleAction = async (id: string, action: 'start' | 'finish') => {
    if(!confirm(action === 'start' ? "Nh·∫≠n vi·ªác n√†y?" : "X√°c nh·∫≠n ho√†n th√†nh?")) return;
    
    let res;
    if (action === 'start') res = await dataSource.startTask(id);
    else res = await dataSource.finishTask(id);

    if (res.success) fetchData(); 
    else alert("L·ªói: " + res.error);
  };

  return (
    <div className={`h-full ${className}`}>
      {!selectedItem && (
        <KhungDanhSach
          data={items}
          tabDefs={filterTabs}
          activeTab={activeTab}
          onTabChange={setActiveTab}
          onSearch={setSearchTerm}
          sortOptions={[]}
          activeSort=""
          onSortChange={() => {}}
          showAddButton={false}
          loading={loading}
        >
          <SanXuatList 
            items={filteredList}
            onClickItem={setSelectedItem}
            onAction={handleAction}
          />
        </KhungDanhSach>
      )}

      {selectedItem && (
        <SanXuatDetail 
          data={selectedItem}
          onClose={() => setSelectedItem(null)}
          onAction={handleAction}
        />
      )}
    </div>
  );
}
</file>

                    <p className="text-white/60 text-sm">S·ªë l∆∞·ª£ng: <span className="text-white font-bold">{sp?.so_luong}</span></p>

                </div>

        </div>

        {/* Action Buttons L·ªõn */}
        <div className="pt-4 border-t border-white/10">
            {data.trang_thai === 'cho_viec' && (

                </button>

            {data.trang_thai === 'dang_lam' && (

                    className="w-full py-4 bg-green-600 hover:bg-green-500 text-white font-bold rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center gap-2 shadow-lg hover:shadow-green-500/20 transition-all animate-pulse"

                    <CheckCircle2 size={20} /> X√ÅC NH·∫¨N HO√ÄN TH√ÄNH

<file path="app/components/cacchucnang/sanxuat/SanXuatList.tsx">
"use client";

import React from "react";
import { Clock, Package, User, PlayCircle, CheckCircle2 } from "lucide-react";
import { KeHoachSanXuat, TRANG_THAI_OPTIONS } from "./config";

interface Props {
  items: KeHoachSanXuat[];
  onClickItem: (item: KeHoachSanXuat) => void;
  onAction: (id: string, action: 'start' | 'finish') => void;
}

export default function SanXuatList({ items, onClickItem, onAction }: Props) {
  if (items.length === 0) {
    return (
      <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-64 text-white/30">
        <Package size={48} className="mb-4 opacity-50" />
        <p>Kh√¥ng c√≥ c√¥ng vi·ªác n√†o.</p>
      </div>
    );
  }

  return (
    <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 xl:grid-cols-4 gap-4 p-4">
      {items.map((item) => {
        const statusConfig = TRANG_THAI_OPTIONS.find(s => s.value === item.trang_thai);
        const StatusIcon = statusConfig?.icon || Clock;
        const isDoing = item.trang_thai === 'dang_lam';
        const isDone = item.trang_thai === 'hoan_thanh';

        return (
          <div 
            key={item.id}
            onClick={() => onClickItem(item)}
            className={`
              group relative p-4 rounded-xl border cursor-pointer transition-all hover:-translate-y-1 hover:shadow-lg
              ${isDoing 
                ? 'bg-[#C69C6D]/10 border-[#C69C6D] shadow-[0_0_15px_rgba(198,156,109,0.2)]' 
                : 'bg-[#0f0f0f] border-white/10 hover:border-white/30'
              }
              ${isDone ? 'opacity-60 grayscale hover:grayscale-0' : ''}
            `}
          >
            {/* Header: M√£ ƒê∆°n & Status */}
            <div className="flex justify-between items-start mb-3">
              <span className="text-[10px] font-mono text-white/50 bg-white/5 px-2 py-1 rounded">
                {item.chi_tiet_don_hang?.don_hang?.ma_don || 'N/A'}
              </span>
              <div className={`flex items-center gap-1 text-xs font-bold ${statusConfig?.color}`}>
                <StatusIcon size={14} />
                <span className="uppercase">{statusConfig?.label}</span>
              </div>
            </div>

            {/* Content: T√™n Vi·ªác & ·∫¢nh */}
            <div className="flex gap-3 mb-3">
              <div className="w-16 h-16 bg-[#1a1a1a] rounded-lg border border-white/5 overflow-hidden shrink-0">
                {item.chi_tiet_don_hang?.mau_thiet_ke?.hinh_anh ? (
                  <img src={item.chi_tiet_don_hang.mau_thiet_ke.hinh_anh} className="w-full h-full object-cover" />
                ) : (
                  <div className="w-full h-full flex items-center justify-center text-white/10"><Package size={24}/></div>
                )}
              </div>
              <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                <h3 className={`font-bold text-sm line-clamp-2 ${isDoing ? 'text-[#C69C6D]' : 'text-white'}`}>
                  {item.ten_viec}
                </h3>
                <p className="text-xs text-white/50 mt-1 truncate">
                  {item.chi_tiet_don_hang?.ghi_chu_san_pham || "S·∫£n ph·∫©m theo ƒë∆°n"}
                </p>
              </div>
            </div>

            {/* Footer: Th√¥ng tin & N√∫t b·∫•m nhanh */}
            <div className="pt-3 border-t border-white/5 flex items-center justify-between">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-xs text-white/40">
                <span className="flex items-center gap-1"><Clock size={12}/> {item.thoi_gian_du_kien}p</span>
                {item.nguoi_thuc_hien && (
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-1 pl-2 border-l border-white/10">
                    <User size={12}/> {item.nguoi_thuc_hien.ho_ten}
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>

              {/* Action Buttons (ngƒÉn s·ª± ki·ªán click v√†o card) */}
              <div onClick={e => e.stopPropagation()}>
                {item.trang_thai === 'cho_viec' && (
                  <button 
                    onClick={() => onAction(item.id, 'start')}
                    className="p-2 bg-blue-600/20 text-blue-400 rounded-lg hover:bg-blue-600 hover:text-white transition-colors"
                    title="Nh·∫≠n vi·ªác"
                  >
                    <PlayCircle size={18} />
                  </button>
                )}
                {item.trang_thai === 'dang_lam' && (
                  <button 
                    onClick={() => onAction(item.id, 'finish')}
                    className="p-2 bg-green-600/20 text-green-400 rounded-lg hover:bg-green-600 hover:text-white transition-colors animate-pulse"
                    title="Ho√†n th√†nh"
                  >
                    <CheckCircle2 size={18} />
                  </button>
                )}
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        );
      })}
    </div>
  );
}

<file path="app/components/cacchucnang/tacphamtrungbay/config.ts">
import { Image as ImageIcon, Ruler, Layers, PenTool, Palette } from "lucide-react";
import { ManagerConfig, FieldConfig, FilterTabConfig } from "../types";
import { 
    getTacPhamDataAction, 
    createTacPhamAction, 
    updateTacPhamAction, 
    deleteTacPhamAction 
} from "@/app/actions/QuyenHanTacPham";
import { getMauThietKeOptionsAction } from "@/app/actions/QuyenHanQuyTrinhMau"; // T√°i s·ª≠ d·ª•ng h√†m l·∫•y option

export interface TacPhamTrungBay {
    id: string;
    ten_mau_thiet_ke: string;
    hinh_anh?: string;
    kich_thuoc: string;
    chat_lieu: string;
    ky_thuat_thuc_hien: string;
    // D·ªØ li·ªáu form
    mau_thiet_ke?: string;
}

const KICH_THUOC_OPTS = ['20x30', '30x40', '40x60'];
const CHAT_LIEU_OPTS = ['G·∫°o nguy√™n h·∫°t 100%', 'G·∫°o - T·∫•m - C√°m'];
const KY_THUAT_OPTS = ['Th·ªß c√¥ng 100%', 'In UV', 'B√°n th·ªß c√¥ng'];

const fields: FieldConfig[] = [
    {
        key: 'hinh_anh',
        label: 'H√¨nh ·∫£nh',
        type: 'image',
        showInForm: false, // ·∫¢nh l·∫•y t·ª´ m·∫´u thi·∫øt k·∫ø, kh√¥ng up tr·ª±c ti·∫øp ·ªü ƒë√¢y
        showInDetail: true,
        showInCard: true,
    },
    {
        key: 'mau_thiet_ke', // ID ƒë·ªÉ l∆∞u DB
        label: 'M·∫´u Thi·∫øt K·∫ø',
        type: 'select-add',
        placeholder: 'Ch·ªçn m·∫´u...',
        required: true,
        icon: Palette,
        showInCard: false,
        optionsLoader: async () => {
             const res = await getMauThietKeOptionsAction();
             return res.data?.map((m: any) => ({ value: m.id, label: m.label })) || [];
        }
    },
    {
        key: 'ten_mau_thiet_ke', // T√™n ƒë·ªÉ hi·ªÉn th·ªã
        label: 'T√™n T√°c Ph·∫©m',
        type: 'text',
        showInForm: false,
        icon: Palette,
    },
    {
        key: 'kich_thuoc',
        label: 'K√≠ch Th∆∞·ªõc',
        type: 'select',
        options: KICH_THUOC_OPTS,
        required: true,
        icon: Ruler,
    },
    {
        key: 'chat_lieu',
        label: 'Ch·∫•t Li·ªáu',
        type: 'select',
        options: CHAT_LIEU_OPTS,
        required: true,
        icon: Layers,
    },
    {
        key: 'ky_thuat_thuc_hien',
        label: 'K·ªπ Thu·∫≠t',
        type: 'select',
        options: KY_THUAT_OPTS,
        required: true,
        icon: PenTool,
    },
];

const filterTabs: FilterTabConfig[] = [
    { id: 'all', label: 'T·∫§T C·∫¢' },
    { id: 'G·∫°o nguy√™n h·∫°t 100%', label: 'G·∫†O 100%', filterField: 'chat_lieu' },
    { id: 'G·∫°o - T·∫•m - C√°m', label: 'T·∫§M C√ÅM', filterField: 'chat_lieu' },
];

const dataSource = {
    fetchList: async (page: number, limit: number, search: string, filter: string) => {
        const res = await getTacPhamDataAction(page, limit, search, filter);
        return { success: res.success, data: res.data as unknown as TacPhamTrungBay[], error: res.error };
    },
    create: async (data: any) => {
        const res = await createTacPhamAction(data);
        return { success: res.success, data: null, error: res.error };
    },
    update: async (id: string, data: any) => {
        const res = await updateTacPhamAction(id, data);
        return { success: res.success, data: null, error: res.error };
    },
    delete: async (id: string) => {
        const res = await deleteTacPhamAction(id);
        return { success: res.success, error: res.error };
    }
};

export function createTacPhamConfig(): ManagerConfig<TacPhamTrungBay> {
    return {
        entityName: 't√°c ph·∫©m',
        entityNamePlural: 't√°c ph·∫©m tr∆∞ng b√†y',
        idField: 'id',
        fields,
        cardConfig: {
            avatarField: 'hinh_anh',
            titleField: 'ten_mau_thiet_ke',
            subtitleField: 'chat_lieu',
            infoFields: [
                { field: 'kich_thuoc', icon: Ruler },
                { field: 'ky_thuat_thuc_hien', icon: PenTool }
            ]
        },
        filterTabs,
        detailTabs: [{ id: 'info', label: 'TH√îNG TIN' }],
        actions: {
            allowView: true,
            allowEdit: true,
            allowDelete: true,
        },
        dataSource,
        searchFields: ['ten_mau_thiet_ke'],
    };
}

export { default as TacPhamTrungBayChucNang } from './TacPhamTrungBayChucNang';

<file path="app/components/cacchucnang/tacphamtrungbay/TacPhamTrungBayChucNang.tsx">
"use client";

import React, { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from "react";
import { KhungDanhSach, KhungForm, KhungChiTiet } from "@/app/components/cacchucnang/KhungGiaoDienChucNang";
import ConfirmDialog from "@/app/components/ConfirmDialog";
import { createTacPhamConfig, TacPhamTrungBay } from "./config";
import ViecMauList from "../viecmau/ViecMauList"; // T√°i s·ª≠ d·ª•ng Grid Card ƒë·∫πp

interface Props {
    permissions?: any; // C√≥ th·ªÉ m·ªü r·ªông sau
}

export default function TacPhamTrungBayChucNang({ permissions }: Props) {
    const config = createTacPhamConfig();
    
    // State qu·∫£n l√Ω
    const [items, setItems] = useState<TacPhamTrungBay[]>([]);
    const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
    const [viewMode, setViewMode] = useState<'list' | 'form' | 'detail'>('list');
    const [selectedItem, setSelectedItem] = useState<TacPhamTrungBay | null>(null);
    const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState('all');
    const [searchTerm, setSearchTerm] = useState('');
    const [confirmDelete, setConfirmDelete] = useState<{ show: boolean; ids: string[] }>({ show: false, ids: [] });

    // Fetch Data
    const fetchData = useCallback(async () => {
        setLoading(true);
        try {
            const res = await config.dataSource!.fetchList!(1, 100, searchTerm, activeTab);
            if (res.success && res.data) setItems(res.data);
        } catch(e) { console.error(e); }
        finally { setLoading(false); }
    }, [activeTab, searchTerm]);

    useEffect(() => { fetchData(); }, [fetchData]);

    // Handlers
    const handleDelete = async () => {
        if(confirmDelete.ids.length > 0) {
            await config.dataSource!.delete!(confirmDelete.ids[0]);
            setConfirmDelete({ show: false, ids: [] });
            fetchData();
            if(viewMode === 'detail') setViewMode('list');
        }
    };

    return (
        <div className="h-full">
            {/* 1. DANH S√ÅCH */}
            {viewMode === 'list' && (
                <KhungDanhSach
                    data={items}
                    tabDefs={config.filterTabs.map(t => ({...t, id: t.id || '', count: 0}))} // Map ƒë·ªÉ kh·ªõp type
                    activeTab={activeTab}
                    onTabChange={setActiveTab}
                    onSearch={setSearchTerm}
                    onAdd={() => { setSelectedItem(null); setViewMode('form'); }}
                    showAddButton={true}
                    loading={loading}
                >
                    <ViecMauList 
                        items={items.map(i => ({
                            id: i.id,
                            mo_ta: i.ten_mau_thiet_ke,
                            phan_loai: `${i.kich_thuoc} ‚Ä¢ ${i.chat_lieu}`,
                            hinh_anh: i.hinh_anh,
                            tao_luc: '',
                            phan_loai_normalized: ''
                        }))}
                        bulkMode={false}
                        selectedIds={new Set()}
                        onToggleSelect={() => {}}
                        onClickItem={(item) => {
                            const original = items.find(i => i.id === item.id);
                            if(original) {
                                setSelectedItem(original);
                                setViewMode('detail');
                            }
                        }}
                    />
                </KhungDanhSach>
            )}

            {/* 2. FORM */}
            {viewMode === 'form' && (
                <KhungForm
                    title={selectedItem ? "C·∫¨P NH·∫¨T T√ÅC PH·∫®M" : "TH√äM T√ÅC PH·∫®M M·ªöI"}
                    onClose={() => setViewMode('list')}
                    data={selectedItem || {}}
                    action={{
                        validate: (data) => {
                            if(!data.mau_thiet_ke) return "Vui l√≤ng ch·ªçn M·∫´u thi·∫øt k·∫ø";
                            if(!data.kich_thuoc) return "Vui l√≤ng ch·ªçn K√≠ch th∆∞·ªõc";
                            return null;
                        },
                        onSave: async (data) => {
                            if(selectedItem) return config.dataSource!.update!(selectedItem.id, data);
                            return config.dataSource!.create!(data);
                        },
                        onSuccess: () => fetchData()
                    }}
                >
                   {/* Form Render th·ªß c√¥ng ho·∫∑c map */}
                   <div className="grid gap-4">
                        {config.fields.map(field => {
                            if(!field.showInForm && field.key !== 'mau_thiet_ke' && field.key !== 'kich_thuoc' && field.key !== 'chat_lieu' && field.key !== 'ky_thuat_thuc_hien') return null;
                            
                            return (
                                <div key={field.key}>
                                    <label className="text-xs text-gray-400 font-bold uppercase mb-1 block">{field.label}</label>
                                    
                                    {/* Select Add (Async) */}
                                    {field.type === 'select-add' ? (
                                         // üü¢ NOTE: T·∫°m d√πng Select th∆∞·ªùng, sau n√†y thay b·∫±ng component AsyncSelect x·ªãn
                                        <AsyncSelectWrapper loader={field.optionsLoader} name={field.key} defaultValue={selectedItem?.mau_thiet_ke} />
                                    ) : field.type === 'select' ? (
                                        <select name={field.key} 
                                            className="w-full bg-[#1a1a1a] border border-white/10 p-3 rounded text-white outline-none focus:border-[#C69C6D]"
                                            defaultValue={(selectedItem as any)?.[field.key] || ""}
                                            onChange={(e) => {
                                                // Logic onChange s·∫Ω ƒë∆∞·ª£c KhungForm x·ª≠ l√Ω n·∫øu truy·ªÅn ƒë√∫ng, 
                                                // ·ªü ƒë√¢y ta ƒëang render custom children n√™n c·∫ßn manual state update ·ªü KhungForm 
                                                // (Ph·∫ßn n√†y KhungForm ƒë√£ handle qua cloneElement ho·∫∑c context, t·∫°m th·ªùi ƒë·ªÉ ƒë∆°n gi·∫£n ta d√πng uncontrolled)
                                            }}
                                        >
                                            {field.options?.map((opt: any) => (
                                                <option key={opt} value={opt}>{opt}</option>
                                            ))}
                                        </select>
                                    ) : null}
                                </div>
                            )
                        })}
                   </div>
                   
                   {/* ‚ö†Ô∏è L∆ØU √ù: KhungForm hi·ªán t·∫°i c·∫ßn n√¢ng c·∫•p ƒë·ªÉ support render children input t·ª± ƒë·ªông bind state. 
                       T·∫°m th·ªùi component n√†y d√πng uncontrolled inputs (name attribute) ƒë·ªÉ KhungForm l·∫•y data qua FormData ho·∫∑c state ngo√†i.
                       ƒê·ªÉ code ch·∫°y ngay, b·∫°n n√™n copy logic Input/Select t·ª´ ViecMauForm.tsx sang ƒë√¢y. */}
                </KhungForm>
            )}

            {/* 3. DETAIL */}
            {viewMode === 'detail' && selectedItem && (
                 <KhungChiTiet
                    data={selectedItem}
                    onClose={() => setViewMode('list')}
                    title={selectedItem.ten_mau_thiet_ke}
                    tabDefs={[{ id: 'info', label: 'TH√îNG TIN' }]}
                    showEditButton={true}
                    showDeleteButton={true}
                    onEdit={() => setViewMode('form')}
                    onDelete={() => setConfirmDelete({ show: true, ids: [selectedItem.id] })}
                 >
                    <div className="p-4 space-y-4">
                        <div className="aspect-video bg-[#1a1a1a] rounded overflow-hidden border border-white/10">
                            {selectedItem.hinh_anh ? (
                                <img src={selectedItem.hinh_anh} className="w-full h-full object-contain" />
                            ) : (
                                <div className="w-full h-full flex items-center justify-center text-white/20">Ch∆∞a c√≥ ·∫£nh</div>
                            )}
                        </div>
                        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
                            <InfoBox label="K√≠ch th∆∞·ªõc" value={selectedItem.kich_thuoc} />
                            <InfoBox label="Ch·∫•t li·ªáu" value={selectedItem.chat_lieu} />
                            <InfoBox label="K·ªπ thu·∫≠t" value={selectedItem.ky_thuat_thuc_hien} />
                        </div>
                    </div>
                 </KhungChiTiet>
            )}

            <ConfirmDialog 
                isOpen={confirmDelete.show}
                title="X√ÅC NH·∫¨N X√ìA"
                message="B·∫°n c√≥ ch·∫Øc ch·∫Øn mu·ªën x√≥a t√°c ph·∫©m n√†y?"
                onConfirm={handleDelete}
                onCancel={() => setConfirmDelete({ show: false, ids: [] })}
            />
        </div>
    );
}

// Component ph·ª• ƒë·ªÉ load options async
function AsyncSelectWrapper({ loader, name, defaultValue }: any) {
    const [opts, setOpts] = useState<any[]>([]);
    useEffect(() => {
        loader().then((res: any) => setOpts(res));
    }, []);

    // üü¢ S·ª≠a l·∫°i logic render form ·ªü phi√™n b·∫£n sau cho m∆∞·ª£t h∆°n
    // ·ªû ƒë√¢y d√πng select native cho nhanh g·ªçn
    return (
        <select name={name} defaultValue={defaultValue || ""} className="w-full bg-[#1a1a1a] border border-white/10 p-3 rounded text-white outline-none focus:border-[#C69C6D]">
            <option value="" disabled>-- Ch·ªçn m·∫´u --</option>
            {opts.map((o) => (
                <option key={o.value} value={o.value}>{o.label}</option>
            ))}
        </select>
    )
}

function InfoBox({ label, value }: any) {
    return (
        <div className="bg-[#1a1a1a] p-3 rounded border border-white/5">
            <div className="text-[10px] text-gray-500 uppercase font-bold mb-1">{label}</div>
            <div className="text-white font-medium">{value}</div>
        </div>
    );
}

<file path="app/components/cacchucnang/viecmau/ViecMauChucNang.tsx">
"use client";

import React, { useState, useEffect, useMemo, useCallback } from "react";
import { Trash2, User, Tag, Calendar, ClipboardList } from "lucide-react";
import {
  KhungDanhSach,
  KhungChiTiet,
} from "@/app/components/cacchucnang/KhungGiaoDienChucNang";
import ConfirmDialog from "@/app/components/ConfirmDialog";
import {
  ViecMau,
  ViecMauPermissions,
  createViecMauConfig,
} from "./config";

// Import c√°c sub-components
import ViecMauList from "./ViecMauList";
import ViecMauForm from "./ViecMauForm";

interface Props {
  permissions?: ViecMauPermissions;
  className?: string;
}

// Helper t√¨m ki·∫øm ti·∫øng Vi·ªát kh√¥ng d·∫•u
const toNonAccent = (str: string) =>
  str
    .normalize("NFD")
    .replace(/[\u0300-\u036f]/g, "")
    .replace(/\s+/g, "")
    .toLowerCase();

export default function ViecMauChucNang({
  permissions = {},
  className = "",
}: Props) {
  const config = createViecMauConfig(permissions);
  const {
    allowEdit = true,
    allowDelete = false,
    allowBulk = false,
  } = permissions;

  // --- STATE ---
  const [items, setItems] = useState<ViecMau[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [searchTerm, setSearchTerm] = useState("");
  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState("all");
  const [sortBy, setSortBy] = useState("newest");

  // View Mode
  const [viewMode, setViewMode] = useState<"list" | "detail" | "form">("list");
  const [selectedItem, setSelectedItem] = useState<ViecMau | null>(null);

  // Bulk Action
  const [bulkMode, setBulkMode] = useState(false);
  const [selectedIds, setSelectedIds] = useState<Set<string>>(new Set());
  const [confirmDelete, setConfirmDelete] = useState<{
    show: boolean;
    ids: string[];
  }>({ show: false, ids: [] });

  // --- FETCH DATA ---
  const fetchData = useCallback(async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      if (config.dataSource?.fetchList) {
        // L·∫•y 1000 d√≤ng ƒë·ªÉ filter client cho m∆∞·ª£t (v·ªõi b·∫£ng danh m·ª•c n√†y th∆∞·ªùng √≠t d·ªØ li·ªáu)
        const res = await config.dataSource.fetchList(1, 1000, "", "");
        if (res.success && res.data) setItems(res.data);
      }
    } catch (e) {
      console.error(e);
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  }, [config.dataSource]);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchData();
  }, [fetchData]);

  // --- FILTER & SORT ---
  const filteredList = useMemo(() => {
    let result = items;

    // Filter Tab
    if (activeTab !== "all") {
      result = result.filter((i) => i.phan_loai_normalized === activeTab);
    }

    // Search
    if (searchTerm) {
      const term = toNonAccent(searchTerm);
      result = result.filter((i) => toNonAccent(i.mo_ta).includes(term));
    }

    // Sort
    const sortOpt = config.sortOptions?.find((s) => s.key === sortBy);
    if (sortOpt?.sortFn) {
      result = [...result].sort(sortOpt.sortFn);
    }

    return result;
  }, [items, activeTab, searchTerm, sortBy, config.sortOptions]);

  // Config Tabs cho KhungDanhSach (ƒë·ªÉ t·ª± ƒë·∫øm s·ªë l∆∞·ª£ng)
  const listTabDefs = useMemo(() => {
    return config.filterTabs.map((t) => ({
      id: t.id || "",
      label: t.label,
      filterField: t.filterField,
    }));
  }, [config.filterTabs]);

  // --- HANDLERS ---
  const handleOpenDetail = (item: ViecMau) => {
    setSelectedItem(item);
    setViewMode("detail");
  };

  const handleOpenForm = (item?: ViecMau) => {
    setSelectedItem(item || null);
    setViewMode("form");
  };

  const handleDelete = async (ids: string[]) => {
    if (config.dataSource?.delete) {
      for (const id of ids) await config.dataSource.delete(id);
      await fetchData();
      setSelectedIds(new Set());
      setConfirmDelete({ show: false, ids: [] });
      if (viewMode === "detail") setViewMode("list");
    }
  };

  const handleBulkSelect = (id: string) => {
    const newSet = new Set(selectedIds);
    if (newSet.has(id)) newSet.delete(id);
    else newSet.add(id);
    setSelectedIds(newSet);
  };

  // --- RENDER ---
  return (
    <div className={`h-full ${className}`}>
      {/* 1. DANH S√ÅCH */}
      {viewMode === "list" && (
        <KhungDanhSach
          data={items}
          tabDefs={listTabDefs}
          activeTab={activeTab}
          onTabChange={setActiveTab}
          onSearch={setSearchTerm}
          sortOptions={
            config.sortOptions?.map((s) => ({ key: s.key, label: s.label })) ||
            []
          }
          activeSort={sortBy}
          onSortChange={setSortBy}
          showAddButton={allowEdit}
          onAdd={() => handleOpenForm()}
          bulkMode={bulkMode}
          onBulkModeToggle={
            allowBulk ? () => setBulkMode(!bulkMode) : undefined
          }
          selectedCount={selectedIds.size}
          onSelectAll={() =>
            setSelectedIds(new Set(filteredList.map((i) => i.id)))
          }
          onClearSelection={() => setSelectedIds(new Set())}
          bulkActions={
            allowDelete
              ? [
                  {
                    id: "delete",
                    label: "X√ìA",
                    icon: Trash2,
                    color: "danger",
                    onClick: () =>
                      setConfirmDelete({
                        show: true,
                        ids: Array.from(selectedIds),
                      }),
                  },
                ]
              : []
          }
          loading={loading}
        >
          <ViecMauList
            items={filteredList}
            bulkMode={bulkMode}
            selectedIds={selectedIds}
            onToggleSelect={handleBulkSelect}
            onClickItem={handleOpenDetail}
          />
        </KhungDanhSach>
      )}

      {/* 2. FORM (TH√äM/S·ª¨A) */}
      {viewMode === "form" && (
        <ViecMauForm
          data={selectedItem}
          onClose={() => {
            setViewMode("list");
            setSelectedItem(null);
          }}
          onSuccess={() => {
            fetchData();
            setViewMode("list");
            setSelectedItem(null);
          }}
        />
      )}

      {/* 3. CHI TI·∫æT */}
      {viewMode === "detail" && selectedItem && (
        <KhungChiTiet
          data={selectedItem}
          onClose={() => {
            setViewMode("list");
            setSelectedItem(null);
          }}
          title={selectedItem.mo_ta}
          // Tab chi ti·∫øt ƒë∆°n gi·∫£n
          tabDefs={[{ id: "thongtin", label: "TH√îNG TIN" }]}
          activeTab="thongtin"
          showEditButton={allowEdit}
          showDeleteButton={allowDelete}
          onEdit={() => handleOpenForm(selectedItem)}
          onDelete={() =>
            setConfirmDelete({ show: true, ids: [selectedItem.id] })
          }
        >
          <div className="p-4 space-y-4">
            {/* ·∫¢nh l·ªõn */}
            <div className="aspect-video w-full rounded-xl overflow-hidden bg-[#1a1a1a] border border-white/10 flex items-center justify-center">
              {selectedItem.hinh_anh ? (
                <img
                  src={selectedItem.hinh_anh}
                  alt=""
                  className="w-full h-full object-contain"
                />
              ) : (
                <ClipboardList size={64} className="text-white/10" />
              )}
            </div>

            {/* Th√¥ng tin chi ti·∫øt */}
            <div className="space-y-3">
              <DetailRow
                icon={<Tag size={18} />}
                label="Ph√¢n lo·∫°i"
                value={selectedItem.phan_loai}
              />
              <DetailRow
                icon={<User size={18} />}
                label="Ng∆∞·ªùi t·∫°o"
                value={selectedItem.nguoi_tao}
              />
              <DetailRow
                icon={<Calendar size={18} />}
                label="Ng√†y t·∫°o"
                value={
                  selectedItem.tao_luc
                    ? new Date(selectedItem.tao_luc).toLocaleDateString("vi-VN")
                    : "---"
                }
              />
            </div>
          </div>
        </KhungChiTiet>
      )}

      {/* CONFIRM DELETE */}
      <ConfirmDialog
        isOpen={confirmDelete.show}
        title="X√ÅC NH·∫¨N X√ìA"
        message={`B·∫°n c√≥ ch·∫Øc mu·ªën x√≥a ${confirmDelete.ids.length} c√¥ng vi·ªác n√†y kh√¥ng?`}
        onConfirm={() => handleDelete(confirmDelete.ids)}
        onCancel={() => setConfirmDelete({ show: false, ids: [] })}
      />
    </div>
  );
}

// Sub-component nh·ªè ƒë·ªÉ hi·ªÉn th·ªã d√≤ng th√¥ng tin trong Chi ti·∫øt
function DetailRow({ icon, label, value }: { icon: any; label: string; value?: string }) {
  return (
    <div className="p-3 bg-[#151515] rounded-xl border border-white/5 flex items-center gap-3">
      <div className="text-[#C69C6D]">{icon}</div>
      <div>
        <p className="text-[10px] text-white/40 font-bold uppercase">{label}</p>
        <p className="text-white text-sm">{value || "---"}</p>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

"use client";

import React, { useState } from "react";
import { KhungForm } from "@/app/components/cacchucnang/KhungGiaoDienChucNang";
import { ViecMau, createViecMauConfig } from "./config";

interface Props {
  data: ViecMau | null; // null = T·∫°o m·ªõi
  onClose: () => void;
  onSuccess: () => void;
}

export default function ViecMauForm({ data, onClose, onSuccess }: Props) {
  const config = createViecMauConfig();
  
  // Kh·ªüi t·∫°o state form
  const [formData, setFormData] = useState<Partial<ViecMau>>(
    data ? { ...data } : {}
  );

  // Helper c·∫≠p nh·∫≠t state
  const handleChange = (field: keyof ViecMau, value: any) => {
    setFormData((prev) => ({ ...prev, [field]: value }));
  };

  return (
    <KhungForm
      isEditing={!!data}
      data={formData}
      onClose={onClose}
      title={data ? "C·∫¨P NH·∫¨T C√îNG VI·ªÜC" : "TH√äM C√îNG VI·ªÜC M·ªöI"}
      
      // C·∫•u h√¨nh Upload ·∫£nh
      avatar={formData.hinh_anh}
      showAvatarUpload={true}
      uploadBucket="images" // Upload v√†o bucket chung
      onUploadComplete={(url) => handleChange("hinh_anh", url)}

      // Logic L∆∞u & Validate
      action={{
        validate: (currData) => {
          if (!currData.mo_ta?.trim()) return "Vui l√≤ng nh·∫≠p T√™n c√¥ng vi·ªác!";
          if (!currData.phan_loai) return "Vui l√≤ng ch·ªçn Ph√¢n lo·∫°i!";
          return null;
        },
        onSave: async (currData) => {
          if (data?.id) {
            return await config.dataSource?.update?.(data.id, currData);
          } else {
            return await config.dataSource?.create?.(currData);
          }
        },
        onSuccess: onSuccess,
      }}
      
      isDirty={true}
    >
      <div className="space-y-4">
        {/* T√™n c√¥ng vi·ªác */}
        <div>
          <label className="text-xs font-bold text-white/60 mb-2 block uppercase">
            T√™n c√¥ng vi·ªác / M√¥ t·∫£ <span className="text-red-500">*</span>
          </label>
          <input
            className="w-full bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-lg px-4 py-3 text-white focus:border-[#C69C6D] outline-none placeholder-white/20"
            value={formData.mo_ta || ""}
            onChange={(e) => handleChange("mo_ta", e.target.value)}
            placeholder="V√≠ d·ª•: ƒê·ªï g·∫°o n·ªÅn size 20x30..."
            autoFocus
          />
        </div>

        {/* Ph√¢n lo·∫°i */}
        <div>
          <label className="text-xs font-bold text-white/60 mb-2 block uppercase">
            Ph√¢n lo·∫°i <span className="text-red-500">*</span>
          </label>
          <div className="relative">
            <select
              className="w-full bg-[#1a1a1a] text-white border border-white/10 rounded-lg px-4 py-3 focus:border-[#C69C6D] outline-none appearance-none"
              value={formData.phan_loai || ""}
              onChange={(e) => handleChange("phan_loai", e.target.value)}
            >
              <option value="" className="text-gray-500">
                -- Ch·ªçn ph√¢n lo·∫°i --
              </option>
              {config.fields
                .find((f) => f.key === "phan_loai")
                ?.options?.map((opt: any) => (
                  <option key={opt} value={opt}>
                    {opt}
                  </option>
                ))}
            </select>
            {/* M≈©i t√™n custom */}
            <div className="absolute right-4 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 pointer-events-none text-white/50 text-xs">
              ‚ñº
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </KhungForm>
  );
}

<file path="app/components/cacchucnang/viecmau/ViecMauList.tsx">
"use client";

import React from "react";
import { ClipboardList, User, Tag } from "lucide-react";
import { ViecMau } from "./config";

interface Props {
  items: ViecMau[];
  bulkMode: boolean;
  selectedIds: Set<string>;
  onToggleSelect: (id: string) => void;
  onClickItem: (item: ViecMau) => void;
}

export default function ViecMauList({
  items,
  bulkMode,
  selectedIds,
  onToggleSelect,
  onClickItem,
}: Props) {
  return (
    <div className="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-4 lg:grid-cols-6 xl:grid-cols-8 gap-3 p-3 md:p-4">
      {items.map((item) => (
        <div
          key={item.id}
          onClick={(e) => {
            if (bulkMode) {
              e.stopPropagation();
              onToggleSelect(item.id);
            } else {
              onClickItem(item);
            }
          }}
          className={`
            group relative bg-[#0f0f0f] border border-white/10 rounded-xl overflow-hidden cursor-pointer 
            hover:border-[#C69C6D]/50 hover:shadow-lg transition-all
            ${
              selectedIds.has(item.id)
                ? "border-[#C69C6D] bg-[#C69C6D]/5"
                : ""
            }
          `}
        >
          {/* Checkbox Bulk Mode */}
          {bulkMode && (
            <div className="absolute top-2 right-2 z-10 w-6 h-6 border-2 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center transition-colors border-white/30 bg-black/60 backdrop-blur-sm">
              {selectedIds.has(item.id) && (
                <span className="text-[#C69C6D] font-bold text-sm">‚úì</span>
              )}
            </div>
          )}

          {/* H√¨nh ·∫£nh (Avatar/Thumbnail) */}
          <div className="aspect-[4/3] w-full bg-[#1a1a1a] relative group-hover:opacity-90 transition-opacity flex items-center justify-center border-b border-white/5">
            {item.hinh_anh ? (
              <img
                src={item.hinh_anh}
                alt={item.mo_ta}
                className="w-full h-full object-cover"
                loading="lazy"
              />
            ) : (
              <div className="flex flex-col items-center gap-2 text-white/10">
                <ClipboardList size={32} strokeWidth={1.5} />
              </div>
            )}
            
            {/* Badge Ph√¢n lo·∫°i n·ªïi l√™n tr√™n h√¨nh */}
            {item.phan_loai && (
              <div className="absolute bottom-2 left-2 bg-black/60 backdrop-blur-sm px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-[9px] font-bold text-white/90 border border-white/10 uppercase tracking-wide">
                {item.phan_loai}
              </div>
            )}
          </div>

          {/* N·ªôi dung th√¥ng tin */}
          <div className="p-3">
            <h3 className="font-bold text-white text-xs md:text-sm line-clamp-2 leading-snug min-h-[2.5em]">
              {item.mo_ta}
            </h3>
            
            <div className="mt-2 pt-2 border-t border-white/5 flex items-center justify-between text-[10px] text-white/40">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-1">
                <User size={10} />
                <span className="truncate max-w-[80px]">
                  {item.nguoi_tao || "---"}
                </span>
              </div>
              {/* C√≥ th·ªÉ th√™m ng√†y t·∫°o ho·∫∑c th√¥ng tin kh√°c ·ªü ƒë√¢y n·∫øu c·∫ßn */}
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
}
